[30;1m467 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m469 | [0m[35m[pre-commit hooks](https://git-scm.com/docs/githooks).[0m
[30;1m470 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m472 | [0m[35mto the `.pre-commit-config.yaml` in your repository:[0m
